through a coordinated system spanning kubelet network management, pod sandbox creation, runtime interfaces, and CRI (Container Runtime Interface) specifications.\\n\\n## Core CNI Integration Components:\\n\\n### 1. Pod Creation and Network Setup Orchestration\\nThe primary entry point is Kubelet.SyncPod (pkg/kubelet/kubelet.go), which calls kubeGenericRuntimeManager.SyncPod (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go). When a pod needs network setup, SyncPod calls createPodSandbox (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go) which initiates the CNI plugin invocation chain.\\n\\n### 2. Pod Sandbox Configuration and Network Namespace Setup\\nThe createPodSandbox function (line 41 of kuberuntime_sandbox.go) calls generatePodSandboxConfig to build the PodSandboxConfig structure. This config includes:\\n- Network namespace mode via runtimeutil.NamespacesForPod (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/util/util.go, line 107)\\n- NetworkNamespaceForPod (line 78) determines whether to use NODE or POD network namespace\\n- DNS configuration via runtimeHelper.GetPodDNS (pkg/kubelet/kubelet_network.go, line 69)\\n- Port mappings from container specs\\n- Hostname and domain generation\\n\\n### 3. CNI Plugin Invocation\\nThe generated PodSandboxConfig is passed to runtimeService.RunPodSandbox, which is defined in the CRI service interface (staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go, line 72 in PodSandboxManager interface). The actual CNI plugin invocation happens in the container runtime shim (containerd, docker, cri-o) implementation, not directly in kubernetes/kubernetes. The kubelet delegates to the runtime via this CRI interface.\\n\\n### 4. IP Address Management (IPAM)\\nAfter the pod sandbox is created, the IPAM process is handled by the CNI plugins themselves. The kubelet retrieves the assigned IP addresses via determinePodSandboxIPs (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_sandbox.go, line 313), which reads the Network field from PodSandboxStatus returned by the runtime. The pod status includes the IP address assigned by CNI plugins.\\n\\n### 5.
